harirityanuvartate | dadAtIti sheShaH | anyagaH pApagaH | idaJNchApyatigopyatvAt.h yasmaikasmaichananavAchyamiti bhAvenAha || rahasyametaditi || j~nAnasthitenarUpeNetyAdyuktametat.h devAnAM rahasyaM daivataiH gopyam.h | anyeShAmapyetAdR^ishaj~nAnasatvekathametaddevAnAM rahasyamityata Aha || viduriti || mAnuShAH svarganarakahetu | puNyapAparUpaM kamareti viduH | tasmAddevarahasyatvAdetat.h j~nAnAdisthitarUpeNa muktyAdidAnarUpaM viShNoH karma etajjaneShu sAdhAraNajaneShu na prakAshayedityarthaH | ekAntesaMmantraNekiM prayojanamityata Aha || ata eveti || yadvAtraivaitadupAniShadgatamavaShyambhakamAha || ata eveti || yato janeShu na prakAshayedata evetyarthaH | kamarhaivatadUchaturityAdAvuktakarmashabdArthamAha || karmanAmAtviti || anena puNyena karmaNetyuktakarmashabdopi vyAkhyAtaH | puNyena pApenetyetat.h puNyasthena pApasthena hariNeti vyAkhyAtam.h | tatra puNyapApashabdau nirvakti || pAtanAditi || tatashchAyaMkhaNDArthaH || B-18
